NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
SAEHAESUNG STAMPING AND WELDING PRIVATE LIMITED
Old No. 2/150, New No. 2/297, F Block-401,
ETA Star Jasmine Court,
Mount Poonamallee High Road,
Kattupakkam, Chennai.
Notice of Extraordinary General Meeting
Minutes of the EXTRAORDINARY GENERAL MEETING OF THE MEMBERS of the company held at the Registered office
of the company on Friday the 18th November 2011 at 10.00 A.M.
The following members were present:—
(i)

Mr. KWON OH KEUN.

(ii) Mr. YOVAN (REPRESENTING SAEHAESUNG CO., LTD., KOREA.)
MR. KWON OH KEUN was elected Chairman of the meeting.
(i)

The following Resolution was passed as Special Resolution.
“Resolved that pursuant to Section 484(1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956, that the company be wound-up by the
members voluntarily.

(ii) The following Resolution was passed as Ordinary Resolution.
“Resolved that Mr. KWON OH KEUN, be appointed as liquidator of the company and his remuneration is fixed at
Rs. 5,000/-per month plus out of Pocket Expenses.”
The Meeting terminated with a vote of thanks to the Chair.
Chennai-600 056,
24th November 2011.

KWON OH KEUN,
Chairman.
